payout if the Company does not achieve growth in operating income in 2014.&#160;Operating income is measured on a consolidated or geographic business unit level, as applicable to each named executive officer&#8217;s award. For Messrs. Thompson, Fenton and Bensen  and Ms. Santona the team performance factor measures corporate performance.&#160;For Mr.&#160;Goare, the team performance factor will be based on a combination of the performance of Europe and corporate performance.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">Individual performance will be measured against various qualitative performance factors, including setting and achieving goals that are in line with the Company&#8217;s strategic focus.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">The maximum TIP award that any of the named executive officers can earn in 2014 is 250% of the target award.</font></div><br><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s1E809800CD6553D387027C9071B7C7C6"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 7.01.
